31  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
32  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
33  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
34  import java.nio.charset.CharacterCodingException;
35  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
36  import sun.nio.cs.ext.*;
37  
38  
39  public class IBM930_OLD extends Charset implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
40  {
41  
42      public IBM930_OLD() {
43          super("x-IBM930_Old", null);
44      }
45  
46      public String historicalName() {
47          return "Cp930";
48      }
49  
50      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
51          return (cs instanceof IBM930);
52      }
53  
54      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
55          return new Decoder(this);
56      }
57  
58      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
59          return new Encoder(this);
60      }
61  
62  
63      /**
64       * These accessors are temporarily supplied while sun.io
65       * converters co-exist with the sun.nio.cs.{ext} charset coders
66       * These facilitate sharing of conversion tables between the
67       * two co-existing implementations. When sun.io converters
68       * are made extinct these will be unncessary and should be removed
69       */
70  
71      public String getDecoderSingleByteMappings() {
72          return Decoder.singleByteToChar;
73  
74      }
75  
76      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
77          return Decoder.index1;
78      }
79  
80      public String getDecoderIndex2() {
81          return Decoder.index2;
82  
83      }
84  
85      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
86          return Encoder.index1;
87  
88      }
89      public String getEncoderIndex2() {
90          return Encoder.index2;
91  
92      }
93      public String getEncoderIndex2a() {
94          return Encoder.index2a;
95  
96      }
97  
98      protected static class Decoder extends DBCS_IBM_EBCDIC_Decoder {
99  
100         public Decoder(Charset cs) {
101                 super(cs);
102                 super.mask1 = 0xFFC0;
103                 super.mask2 = 0x003F;
104                 super.shift = 6;
105                 super.singleByteToChar = this.singleByteToChar;
106                 super.index1 = this.index1;
107                 super.index2 = this.index2;
108         }
109
